namespace = dg_church_influence
country_event = {
	id = dg_church_influence.001
	title = dg_church_influence.001.t
	desc = dg_church_influence.001.d
	picture = all_funeral
	trigger = {
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			religion_group = muslim
		}
		NOT = {
			government = theocracy
		}
		NOT = {
			government = native
		}
		NOT = {
			check_variable = {
				which = church_property
				value = 13
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = national_church
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
			}
		}
		OR = {
			piety = -0.60
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				PAP = {
					check_variable = {
						which = papal_authority
						value = 500
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 41
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = dead_hand
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = {
				which = church_property
				value = 7
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = {
				which = church_property
				value = 9
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = church_property
					value = 3
				}
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = church_property
					value = 5
				}
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			is_at_war = yes
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			at_war_with_religious_enemy = yes
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						culture_group = owner
						is_core = owner
						is_capital = no
						is_overseas = no
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owned_by = ROOT
							has_owner_religion = yes
							culture_group = owner
							is_core = owner
							is_capital = no
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_core = owner
						is_capital = no
						is_overseas = no
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owned_by = ROOT
							has_owner_religion = yes
							is_core = owner
							is_capital = no
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_core = owner
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owned_by = ROOT
							has_owner_religion = yes
							is_core = owner
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owned_by = ROOT
							has_owner_religion = yes
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						culture_group = owner
						is_core = owner
						is_capital = no
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_core = owner
						is_capital = no
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_core = owner
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_province_flag = donated_land
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = donated_land_set
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 10
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
						}
						religion_group = muslim
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 20
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
						}
						religion_group = muslim
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 30
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
						}
						religion_group = muslim
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 40
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
						}
						religion_group = muslim
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 50
				}
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
						}
						religion_group = muslim
					}
					set_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = donated_land_set
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
				}
				clr_province_flag = donated_land_neighbor
				set_province_flag = donated_land
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.001.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = dead_hand
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = church_property
						value = 3
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = church_property
						value = 5
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = {
					which = church_property
					value = 7
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = {
					which = church_property
					value = 9
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = {
					which = church_property
					value = 11
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = dead_hand
			change_variable = {
				which = church_property
				value = 1
			}
		}
		add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = donated_land
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {

					}

						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_4
				clr_province_flag = donated_land
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = donated_land
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = -3
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						province_event = {
							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_3
				clr_province_flag = donated_land
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = donated_land
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = -2
					}
					hidden_effect = {

							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
				clr_province_flag = donated_land
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = donated_land
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = -1
					}
					hidden_effect = {

							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_1
				clr_province_flag = donated_land
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.001.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

			}

country_event = {
	id = dg_church_influence.002
	title = dg_church_influence.002.t
	desc = dg_church_influence.002.d
	picture = all_church_submission
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = take_advantage_of_reformation
				}
				clr_country_flag = take_advantage_of_reformation
				every_owned_province = {
					clr_province_flag = renaissance_ideas
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.002.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = church_property
				value = -1
			}
			set_country_flag = appropriated_land
		}
		add_patriarch_authority = -0.05
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.002.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = church_property
				value = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = church_land_seized
				}
			}
			add_piety = -0.05
			set_country_flag = church_land_seized
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_powerful
				duration = 3000
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_building = temple
							has_building = temple_heathen
						}
					}
					OR = {
						base_tax = 7
						is_capital = yes
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 5000
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_riots
					duration = 800
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = 6
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						province_event = {
							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_6
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_strong
				duration = 3000
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_building = temple
							has_building = temple_heathen
						}
					}
					OR = {
						base_tax = 9
						is_capital = yes
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 4000
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_riots
					duration = 600
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = 4
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						province_event = {
							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_moderate
				duration = 3000
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_building = temple
							has_building = temple_heathen
						}
					}
					OR = {
						base_tax = 7
						is_capital = yes
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 3000
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_riots
					duration = 400
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = 2
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						province_event = {
							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.20
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_weak
				duration = 3000
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_building = temple
							has_building = temple_heathen
						}
					}
					OR = {
						base_tax = 9
						is_capital = yes
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 2000
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_riots
					duration = 200
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_impotent
				duration = 3000
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_building = temple
							has_building = temple_heathen
						}
					}
					OR = {
						base_tax = 9
						is_capital = yes
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 1000
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = church_property
				value = -2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = appropriated_land
		set_country_flag = appropriated_land_2
		add_patriarch_authority = -0.10
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.003.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.003.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {

				num_of_cities = 60
			}
			random_core_province = {
				limit = {
					is_overseas = no
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = nobles_organizing
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = "nobles_organizing"
					duration = 1825
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = 5
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						province_event = {
							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_cities = 80
			}
			random_core_province = {
				limit = {
					is_overseas = no
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = nobles_organizing
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = "nobles_organizing"
					duration = 1825
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = 5
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						province_event = {
							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.022.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_stability = -3
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = POP_Stability.003
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_emperor_of_china = yes
			}
			add_mandate = -15
		}
		set_country_flag = secularized_theocracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				government = theocracy
			}
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = divine_right
			add_government_reform = delegated_rulers
			add_government_reform = hereditary_elite
			hidden_effect = {
				set_legacy_government = despotic_monarchy
			}
			set_legacy_government = feudal_monarchy
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_church_influence.023
	title = dg_church_influence.023.t
	desc = dg_church_influence.023.d
	picture = all_powerful_advisor
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.40
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				PAP = {
					check_variable = {
						which = papal_authority
						value = 400
					}
				}
			}
		}
		has_advisor = yes
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 83
		modifier = {
			piety = -0.20
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = church_taxes
				}
				set_country_flag = concession_church_taxes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = dg_public_schools
				}
				set_country_flag = concession_public_schools
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = state_supported_church
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = concession_state_supported_church
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					religion = catholic
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = counter_reformation
						has_country_modifier = preparatory_schools
					}
					set_country_flag = concession_jesuit_schools
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
					}
					set_country_flag = concession_pragmatic_sanction
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							which = monastic_decline
							value = 5
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = concession_monastic_decline
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = sunni
						religion = shiite
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = ulama_patronage
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = concession_ulama_patronage
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							religion = sunni
							religion = shiite
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = sufi_patronage
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = concession_sufi_patronage
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							which = monastic_decline
							value = 5
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = concession_monastic_decline
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = orthodox
						religion = coptic
						religion = chaldean
						religion = gnostic
						religion = ibadi
						religion = wahhabi
						religion = jain
						religion = hinduism
						religion = zoroastrian
						religion = vajrayana
						religion = buddhism
						religion = mahayana
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							which = monastic_decline
							value = 5
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = concession_monastic_decline
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = concession_church_property
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.023.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_church_property
			}
			clr_country_flag = concession_church_property
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = church_property
					value = 1
				}
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_monastic_decline
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_monastic_decline
				change_variable = {
					which = monastic_decline
					value = -1
				}
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
			custom_tooltip = reverse_monastic_decline
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_pragmatic_sanction
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_pragmatic_sanction
				clr_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
			custom_tooltip = church_autonomy_revoked
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_state_supported_church
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_state_supported_church
				set_country_flag = state_supported_church
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
			custom_tooltip = state_supported_church
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_church_taxes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_church_taxes
				clr_country_flag = church_taxes
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
			custom_tooltip = church_taxes_revoked
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_ulama_patronage
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_ulama_patronage
				set_country_flag = ulama_patronage
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
			custom_tooltip = ulama_patronage
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_sufi_patronage
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_sufi_patronage
				set_country_flag = sufi_patronage
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
			custom_tooltip = sufi_patronage
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_public_schools
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_public_schools
			}
			remove_country_modifier = dg_public_schools
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = public_religious_schools
				duration = -1
			}
			custom_tooltip = religious_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = concession_jesuit_schools
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = concession_jesuit_schools
			}
			remove_country_modifier = preparatory_schools
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = jesuit_schools
				duration = -1
			}
			custom_tooltip = religious_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.023.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				advisor = inquisitor
			}
			remove_advisor = inquisitor
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				advisor = theologian
			}
			remove_advisor = theologian
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					advisor = theologian
				}
				NOT = {
					advisor = inquisitor
				}
			}
			remove_advisor = random
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

			}

			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}

			add_prestige = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = -2
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = -1
			add_prestige = -1
		}
	}

		name = dg_church_influence.032.e

				NOT = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = colonial_church_strong
				factor = 0.5
			}

				has_country_flag = colonial_church_moderate
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = colonial_church_weak
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {

				PAP = {

					}

				factor = 0

			}

					}
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = totemism_rebels
					size = 0
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					region = central_america_region
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = nahuatl_rebels
					size = 0
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					continent = south_america
					NOT = {
						region = peru_region
					}
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = pantheism_rebels
					size = 0
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					region = peru_region
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = inti_rebels
					size = 0
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_colony = yes
			}

				limit = {
					units_in_province = 1
				}
				change_native_hostileness = 4
			}
			else = {
				add_colonysize = -100
				change_native_hostileness = 2
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = dg_church_influence.053
	title = dg_church_influence.053.t
	desc = dg_church_influence.053.d
	picture = catholic_court
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
		}
		NOT = {
			legitimacy = 70
		}
		OR = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.25
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				PAP = {
					check_variable = {
						which = papal_authority
						value = 400
					}
				}
			}
		}
		government = monarchy
		has_regency = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = divine_right_of_kings
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = distracted_church
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 41
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.80
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = divine_right_of_kings
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.053.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
			}
			add_legitimacy = 32
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						stability = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = 16
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						stability = 0
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
			}
			add_legitimacy = 8
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						stability = -1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
				patriarch_authority = 0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = 4
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						stability = -2
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
				hidden_effect = {

						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 2
		}
	}

							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
						}
						patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.50
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
						}
						patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_corrupt_pious
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
						}
						patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_corrupt_observant
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
				}
				patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
				}
				patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.75
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier

							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.50
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}

						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_pious
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {

						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_observant

				}

					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				patriarch_hostile_observant = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
				}
				patriarch_hostile_pious = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
				}
				patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical

country_event = {
	id = dg_church_influence.059
	title = dg_church_influence.059.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			government = theocracy
		}
		desc = "dg_church_influence_theocracy.059.d"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				government = theocracy
			}
		}
		desc = "dg_church_influence.059.d"
	}
	picture = catholic_crusade
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
		}
		OR = {
			at_war_with_religious_enemy = yes
			AND = {
				is_at_war = yes
				NOT = {
					any_known_country = {
						war_with = ROOT
						NOT = {
							defensive_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			war_exhaustion = 2
			NOT = {
				manpower_percentage = 0.80
			}
			capital_scope = {
				has_siege = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.25
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				PAP = {
					check_variable = {
						which = papal_authority
						value = 400
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = holy_war_declared
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = morale_boost
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = distracted_church
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 41
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.80
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.20
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = holy_war_declared
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_church_influence.059.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = morale_boost
				duration = 500
			}
			add_war_exhaustion = -2
			add_yearly_manpower = 0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = morale_boost
				duration = 400
			}
			add_war_exhaustion = -1.6
			add_yearly_manpower = 0.08
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = morale_boost
				duration = 300
			}
			add_war_exhaustion = -1.2
			add_yearly_manpower = 0.06
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
				patriarch_authority = 0.20
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = morale_boost
				duration = 200
			}
			add_war_exhaustion = -0.8
			add_yearly_manpower = 0.04
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = morale_boost
				duration = 100
			}
			add_war_exhaustion = -0.4
			add_yearly_manpower = 0.02
		}
	}
}

			}

				}
			}
		}

				NOT = {
					religion = catholic
				}
				has_country_flag = national_church
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 80
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 60
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 50
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						piety = -0.20
						patriarch_authority = 0.40
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						piety = -0.60
						patriarch_authority = 0.20
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
			}
			add_legitimacy = -20
			add_republican_tradition = -10
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_powerful
				duration = 3000
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = -16
			add_republican_tradition = -8
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_strong
				duration = 3000
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
			}
			add_legitimacy = -12
			add_republican_tradition = -6
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_moderate
				duration = 3000
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
				patriarch_authority = 0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = -8
			add_republican_tradition = -4
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_weak
				duration = 3000
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = -4
			add_republican_tradition = -2
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_impotent
				duration = 3000
			}
		}
	}
